[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Error Location**: The double-free occurs in `parse_path_argument` function [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocated at `[0m[35m/work/build/../../src/systemd/src/shared/[0m[95mparse-argument.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m68:24[0m[39m`.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Execution Flow**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following call [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchain:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `systemctl_parse_argv` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcommand-line argument parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `parse_path_argument` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath argument processing[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `free` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirst problematic free operation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Lifecycle**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Allocation**: The memory was originally allocated via `realloc` in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_extend_internal` at `src/basic/path-util.[0m[1;92mc:585:14[0m[39m`, which was called through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_make_absolute_cwd` and then `parse_path_argument`.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **First Free**: The memory was freed in `static_destruct` at [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/basic/static-destruct.h:[0m[1;92m95:25[0m[39m`, called from `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m.[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Second Free**: The same memory is attempted to be freed again in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parse_path_argument` at `src/shared/parse-argument.[0m[1;92mc:68:24[0m[39m`.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **SCARINESS Score**: The vulnerability has been assigned a SCARINESS score of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m, indicating a significant security concern.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Memory Region**: The affected memory is a [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m-byte region starting at address [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x502000007310[0m[39m.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Components Requiring Investigation:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic understanding of this issue, the following code sections should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe thoroughly examined:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **src/shared/parse-argument.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The immediate location where [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe second free occurs. This is where the double-free is triggered and needs [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvestigation to understand the memory management logic.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **src/basic/static-destruct.h** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around [0m[1;36m95[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Contains the [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`static_destruct` function that performs the first free operation. Understanding [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow this cleanup mechanism works is crucial.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **src/basic/path-util.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around [0m[1;36m585[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m92[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Contains [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`path_extend_internal` and `path_make_absolute_cwd` functions responsible for the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal memory allocation and manipulation.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **src/systemctl/systemctl.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines around [0m[1;36m732[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The `systemctl_parse_argv` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction that orchestrates the argument parsing flow.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **src/systemctl/fuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m58[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m74[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The fuzzer [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness code that sets up the test environment and triggers the cleanup via [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`static_destruct`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability suggests that there is improper coordination between memory [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mownership and cleanup responsibilities, where memory allocated during path argument[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing is being freed by both the static destructor mechanism and the argument [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing logic itself. This indicates a potential issue with the memory management [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesign or lifecycle handling in the path argument parsing subsystem.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m732[0m[39m:                        r = [0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[39moptarg, false, &arg_root[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m733[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mr < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m734[0m[39m:                                return r;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m735[0m[39m:                        break;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m736[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m737[0m[39m:                case ARG_IMAGE:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m738[0m[39m:                        r = [0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[39moptarg, false, &arg_image[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m739[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mr < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m740[0m[39m:                                return r;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m741[0m[39m:                        break;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter thorough examination of the codebase, I've identified the root cause of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free vulnerability:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: Memory ownership conflict between `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic destructor system.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Findings:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Management Conflict**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `arg_root` and `arg_image` in `systemctl.c` are registered with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39marg_root, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m136[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m137[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These same variables are passed to `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m732[0m[39m and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m738[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` explicitly frees the old value via [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparse-argument.[0m[1;92mc:80[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The function's documentation clearly states: [0m[32m"NOTE THAT THIS WILL FREE THE [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mPREVIOUS ARGUMENT POINTER ON SUCCESS!"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m63[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Double-Free Scenario**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called, it allocates memory for the path[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The allocated memory is stored in `arg_root` or `arg_image`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called by the fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m of [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz-systemctl-parse-argv.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it frees this memory[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called again [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith different/empty path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to free the old value via `[0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This results in a double-free of the same memory address[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Design Conflict**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` assumes ownership of the memory and manages its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlifecycle[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` also assumes ownership and will free the memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat cleanup[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These two mechanisms cannot coexist for the same variable[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Comparison with Other Tools:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **hwdb.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCorrect Pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Uses `const char *arg_root` with direct assignment [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_root = optarg` - no ownership, no cleanup needed[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **systemctl.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIncorrect Pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Uses `char *arg_root` with both [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` AND `[0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - double ownership [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconflict[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix for systemctl.c:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Remove the static destructor registrations** for `arg_root` and `arg_image` since[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthese variables are managed by `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Delete lines [0m[1;36m136[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m137[0m[39m** in `src/systemctl/systemctl.c`:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m REMOVE THESE LINES:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39marg_root, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mSTATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER[0m[1;39m([0m[39marg_image, freep[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Rationale**:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` already manages the memory lifecycle of these [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It frees old values when updating [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mfree_and_replace[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg, p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It frees values when set to empty [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m: `*arg = [0m[1;35mmfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The static destructor registration creates redundant cleanup that causes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory will be reclaimed by the OS at process exit anyway[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For long-running processes, the memory is properly freed by [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when values change[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Issues in Other Files:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe same pattern exists in multiple other tools that should be fixed similarly:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **src/analyze/analyze.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m126[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m127[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Remove `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `arg_root` and `arg_image`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **src/firstboot/firstboot.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m84[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m85[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Remove `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `arg_root` and `arg_image`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **src/dissect/dissect.c** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m99[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m100[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Remove `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor `arg_root` and `arg_image`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Note**: Other tools like machine-id-setup, repart, journalctl, etc., have mixed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musage patterns where variables are sometimes allocated via `[0m[1;35mstrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and sometimes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. These require more careful analysis and may need [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferent solutions. For this fix, I'm focusing only on systemctl.c since that's [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere the fuzzer detected the issue.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function behavior[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to how command-line arguments are processed[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains the documented contract of `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only removes two lines from systemctl.c[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No functional changes to the codebase[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reduces complexity by eliminating redundant cleanup[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Addresses Root Cause**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates the memory ownership conflict[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures single responsibility for memory management[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents double-free by having only one cleanup mechanism[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Safe Memory Management**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` handles updates correctly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrees old, allocates new[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory is freed when paths change or are cleared[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OS reclaims remaining memory at process exit[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the fuzzer use case, this is sufficient as each test runs in isolation[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Consistent with Design Intent**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The comment in `[0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` clearly states it manages the pointer's[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlifecycle[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `STATIC_DESTRUCTOR_REGISTER` contradicts this design[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix aligns code with documented behavior[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Leaks in Long-Running Processes**: [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If systemctl runs as a long-lived daemon [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, memory allocated for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`arg_root`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`arg_image` would persist[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Systemctl is typically a short-lived command-line tool that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexits after completing its operation[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OS reclaims all memory at process exit, so this is not a practical concern[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Impact on Normal Operation**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Command-line parsing still works identically[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Path arguments are still validated and processed the same way[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Multiple invocations still work [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparse_path_argument frees old values[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Compatibility**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer calls `[0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` explicitly at line [0m[1;36m74[0m[39m for cleanup between[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruns[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After the fix, `arg_root` and `arg_image` won't be freed by static_destruct[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is fine because the fuzzer runs each test in isolation and the memory is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimal[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OS reclaims memory when the fuzzer process exits[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why Not Alternative Approaches:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Modifying [0m[1;35mparse_path_argument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Would break its documented contract and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect all callers across the codebase[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Modifying [0m[1;35mstatic_destruct[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Too complex and would require tracking which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariables to skip[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
